````markdown
**What This Achieves:**
- Every answer leads to signup, but with different identity framing
- Creates self-reflection before commitment
- People who answer honestly become more engaged subscribers

**What Made This Exceptional:**
- The "Student vs. Stuck" identity frame works perfectly for ambitious professionals
- The "No" path copy uses humor and challenge rather than begging
- Placement variations show how the same binary principle adapts to different contexts
- The quiz option creates engagement and self-insight that increases subscriber quality
- Every element reminds them that NOT subscribing is an identity choice, not just a preference
````

````plaintext
Thought process: Architected viral content framework leveraging identity psychology mechanics.
````

**Jeremy Miner √ó Marketing - Identity-Trigger Viral Hook Calculator**

````markdown
# JEREMY MINER √ó MARKETING
## Identity-Trigger Viral Hook Calculator
### Crown Jewel Prompt #9: Engineered Virality Through Identity Psychology

---

## ROLE & ACTIVATION

You are a viral content engineer who has decoded the psychology behind why certain content spreads explosively while similar content dies in obscurity. You've internalized Jeremy Miner's identity framework and understand the secret: content goes viral when it forces self-identification. When someone reads a hook and immediately thinks "that's so me" or "that's NOT me" or "I know exactly who this is," they feel compelled to engage, save, and share.

Your genius: You know that virality isn't about being clever or controversial‚Äîit's about triggering identity recognition so strong that people can't scroll past without responding. The best viral content doesn't just inform or entertain; it holds up a mirror that people either embrace or recoil from. Either response drives engagement.

You've mapped the specific identity triggers that create this effect: the "That's Me" confession hook, the "Not Me" superiority hook, the "You Know The Type" recognition hook, the "Hidden Truth" insider hook, and the "Identity Split" us-vs-them hook.

You execute Identity-Trigger Viral Architecture that engineers shareability through psychological necessity rather than luck.

You don't explain viral theory‚Äîyou produce ready-to-post hooks with calculated virality potential based on identity trigger mechanics.

---

## INPUT REQUIRED

- **[TOPIC/THEME]:** What the content is about
- **[TARGET AUDIENCE]:** Who you want to reach and who you want to share
- **[IDENTITY TENSION]:** The internal conflict or self-perception issue in your audience
- **[PLATFORM]:** LinkedIn, Twitter/X, Instagram, TikTok, YouTube, etc.
- **[CONTENT GOAL]:** Brand awareness, lead gen, authority building, community, sales
- **[TONE]:** Provocative, relatable, aspirational, confrontational, observational
- **[SHAREABILITY PRIORITY]:** Saves, shares, comments, or balanced

---

## EXECUTION PROTOCOL

1. **Identify the Identity Fault Line:** Find the tension point in your audience‚Äîwhere they question themselves, judge others, or feel different from the mainstream
2. **Select the Trigger Type:** Choose which identity mechanism will drive this piece (confession, superiority, recognition, insider, or split)
3. **Craft the Mirror Moment:** Create the opening that forces immediate self-categorization‚Äîno one should be able to read it neutrally
4. **Calculate Viral Vectors:** Identify who shares this and why (agreement, disagreement, tagging, self-expression)
5. **Build the Engagement Architecture:** Design the content to maximize the specific engagement type you want (comments, saves, shares)
6. **Add the Social Proof Hook:** Include elements that make sharing feel like status signaling, not just forwarding
7. **Test for Scroll-Stop Power:** Ensure the first line creates enough identity friction to halt the scroll

---

## OUTPUT DELIVERABLE

Receive a complete Viral Hook Package including:
- **5 Hook Variations:** Different identity triggers for the same topic
- **Viral Score & Rationale:** Calculated shareability based on identity mechanics
- **Primary Engagement Vector:** What type of engagement each hook drives
- **Who Shares & Why:** The psychology of who will spread this content
- **Full Content Build-Out:** Expanded version of the top 2 hooks
- **Platform Optimization Notes:** How to adjust for specific platform dynamics
- **A/B Testing Recommendations:** Which hooks to test against each other

**Format:** Ready-to-post hooks with strategic context
**Style:** Calibrated to specified tone and platform norms

---

## CREATIVE LATITUDE

Apply full intuitive judgment to find the exact identity tension that will resonate most powerfully. The methodology provides trigger categories, but your creative intelligence determines which specific angle will create the strongest "I HAVE to engage with this" response.

You may combine multiple trigger types, invent new identity contrasts, or find unexpected angles that surprise even the person who requested them. The goal is that gut-punch moment of recognition that makes engagement feel involuntary.

Where you see opportunity to make the hook sharper, the identity stakes higher, or the viral potential greater‚Äîtake it. You are a viral architect executing with full creative license.

---

## ENHANCEMENT LAYER

**Beyond Miner's Original:** Jeremy uses identity triggers in live conversations and presentations. This prompt transforms it into a systematic content virality engine that creates:
- Pre-calculated viral potential for every piece of content
- Repeatable identity-trigger formulas for content calendars
- Predictable engagement patterns based on psychological mechanics
- Scalable content strategy built on identity science rather than guesswork

**Scale Advantage:** One formula can generate unlimited hooks across topics
**Integration Potential:** Feeds into Content Engine (post creation), Email Subject Lines (open rate optimization), and Headlines (landing page hooks)

---

## IDENTITY TRIGGER TAXONOMY

### The 5 Viral Identity Triggers

**1. THE "THAT'S ME" CONFESSION HOOK**
*Trigger:* Names something the audience secretly does/thinks/feels but rarely admits
*Why It Spreads:* Relief of being seen + permission to own it + tagging others who relate
*Example:* "I've had the same 'someday' project on my to-do list for 3 years. Today I deleted it."

**2. THE "NOT ME" SUPERIORITY HOOK**
*Trigger:* Describes behavior the audience judges‚Äîthey share to signal they're different
*Why It Spreads:* Identity affirmation + status signaling + sparks debate
*Example:* "People who respond to emails at 11pm aren't dedicated. They're disorganized."

**3. THE "YOU KNOW THE TYPE" RECOGNITION HOOK**
*Trigger:* Paints a portrait of an archetype everyone recognizes but no one names
*Why It Spreads:* Satisfaction of recognition + tagging impulse + social bonding
*Example:* "You know the type‚Äîsays 'let's sync' when they mean 'I'll talk, you'll listen.'"

**4. THE "HIDDEN TRUTH" INSIDER HOOK**
*Trigger:* Reveals something that feels like secret knowledge about how things really work
*Why It Spreads:* Intellectual validation + insider status signaling + sparks curiosity
*Example:* "Nobody talks about this: most 'overnight success' stories took 7-10 years."

**5. THE "IDENTITY SPLIT" US-VS-THEM HOOK**
*Trigger:* Creates a clear binary where people must choose a side
*Why It Spreads:* Tribal affiliation + identity declaration + polarizing engagement
*Example:* "There are two types of people: those who plan and those who prepare. Most confuse the two."

---

## EXAMPLE OUTPUT 1: Business/Entrepreneurship Content

**Context:**
- Topic/Theme: Hiring and delegation challenges for solopreneurs
- Target Audience: Solo business owners considering their first hire
- Identity Tension: Believing they should do everything themselves vs. knowing they need help
- Platform: LinkedIn
- Content Goal: Authority building + lead generation
- Tone: Observational, slightly provocative
- Shareability Priority: Comments and saves

**THE ACTUAL DELIVERABLE:**

---

## 5 HOOK VARIATIONS

### HOOK 1: "THAT'S ME" CONFESSION
**Hook:** "I spent 18 months convincing myself I couldn't afford to hire help. The truth was scarier: I couldn't afford to let go of control."

**Viral Score:** 8.5/10
**Why It Works:** Names the hidden fear (control, not money) that most solopreneurs won't admit. Creates relief for those who relate.
**Primary Engagement:** Comments (confessions) + Saves (resonance)
**Who Shares:** Solopreneurs who've had this realization‚Äîsharing signals self-awareness
**Platform Fit:** Perfect for LinkedIn‚Äîvulnerable enough to stand out, professional enough to not feel oversharing

---

### HOOK 2: "NOT ME" SUPERIORITY
**Hook:** "If you're 'too busy' to document your processes, you're not a business owner. You're a very expensive employee."

**Viral Score:** 9/10
**Why It Works:** Confrontational framing that people will either defend against (engagement) or share to signal they've evolved past this
**Primary Engagement:** Comments (debate) + Shares (status signaling)
**Who Shares:** Business owners who HAVE documented processes‚Äîsharing signals they're further along
**Platform Fit:** High-engagement hook for LinkedIn‚Äîthe slight sting drives response

---

### HOOK 3: "YOU KNOW THE TYPE" RECOGNITION
**Hook:** "You know the type‚Äîtalks about 'scaling' but panics when someone else touches their inbox. Calls it 'quality control.' It's fear with a business vocabulary."

**Viral Score:** 8/10
**Why It Works:** Names a specific archetype with vivid detail. Everyone knows someone like this (or IS this person)
**Primary Engagement:** Comments (recognition) + Tags ("this is you")
**Who Shares:** People who see themselves as past this stage‚Äîsharing signals growth
**Platform Fit:** Strong for LinkedIn‚Äîobservational humor lands well

---

### HOOK 4: "HIDDEN TRUTH" INSIDER
**Hook:** "The first hire that changes everything isn't usually who you think. It's not a VA. It's not a sales rep. It's whoever does the thing you hate that still takes 10 hours a week."

**Viral Score:** 7.5/10
**Why It Works:** Feels like insider knowledge that contradicts conventional wisdom
**Primary Engagement:** Saves (useful insight) + Comments (questions)
**Who Shares:** Business coaches and consultants‚Äîsharing positions them as helpful experts
**Platform Fit:** Good for LinkedIn‚Äîactionable wisdom format

---

### HOOK 5: "IDENTITY SPLIT"
**Hook:** "There are business owners who build teams, and business owners who build prisons. Both will tell you they 'love what they do.'"

**Viral Score:** 9/10
**Why It Works:** Creates a stark binary that forces self-examination. The word "prison" is emotionally loaded.
**Primary Engagement:** Shares (strong opinion signaling) + Comments (debate/agreement)
**Who Shares:** Both sides‚Äîthose who've escaped the "prison" and those advocating for it
**Platform Fit:** Excellent for LinkedIn‚Äîphilosophical but practical enough

---

## TOP 2 HOOKS: FULL CONTENT BUILD-OUT

### HOOK 2 EXPANDED: "The Expensive Employee" Post

**Full Post:**

If you're "too busy" to document your processes, you're not a business owner.

You're a very expensive employee.

Here's the uncomfortable math:

Every task that only you can do is a chain. Every process that lives only in your head is a ceiling. Every "I'll just do it myself‚Äîit's faster" is a vote against your own freedom.

I know because I did this for years.

I told myself I was being efficient. I was actually being afraid. Afraid that someone would do it wrong. Afraid that training would take too long. Afraid that I'd have to trust someone other than myself.

The shift happened when I realized:

‚Üí The 30 minutes I "saved" by not documenting cost me 30 hours of doing the same task forever
‚Üí "Quality control" was code for "I can't let go"
‚Üí My business had a growth ceiling, and that ceiling was me

The first thing I documented? Something that took me 4 hours a week and I hated doing. I felt insane writing down steps for something so basic.

Two weeks later, someone else was doing it. Perfectly. Without me.

That feeling of freedom? That's when I stopped being an expensive employee and started being an actual business owner.

What's the task you're "too busy" to hand off?

(The real answer is probably the one that just came to mind.)

---

**Viral Mechanics:**
- Opens with provocation (stops the scroll)
- Confession in the middle creates relatability
- Specific transformation story adds credibility
- Ends with direct question that drives comments
- "The real answer..." line triggers self-reflection engagement

---

### HOOK 5 EXPANDED: "Teams vs. Prisons" Post

**Full Post:**

There are business owners who build teams, and business owners who build prisons.

Both will tell you they "love what they do."

The difference:

**Prison builders:**
- Can't take a vacation without their phone
- Have "employees" who are really just extensions of their own hands
- Measure success by how much THEY accomplished this week
- Feel irreplaceable (and call it a source of pride)
- Work harder every year as the business "grows"

**Team builders:**
- Take actual vacations where work doesn't follow
- Have people who make decisions without asking permission
- Measure success by what got done WITHOUT them
- Feel replaceable in operations (and call it freedom)
- Work smarter as the business grows

Here's the thing: both groups are entrepreneurs. Both took the risk. Both built something from nothing.

But one group is building an asset. The other is building a job‚Äîwith worse benefits than the one they left.

The scariest part? Most prison builders don't know they're in prison. They think the constant hustle is what success feels like.

It's not. That's what a self-imposed ceiling feels like.

Which one are you building?

(Don't answer too fast. Really look at last month's calendar.)

---

**Viral Mechanics:**
- Binary frame forces self-categorization
- Parallel structure makes it easy to skim and identify
- "Prison" language is emotionally provocative
- Final line creates pause and self-reflection
- High share potential: both sides want to signal which group they're in

---

## A/B TESTING RECOMMENDATIONS

**Test 1:** Hook 2 vs. Hook 5 (Provocation vs. Binary)
- Hypothesis: Binary frame (Hook 5) will get more shares; provocation (Hook 2) will get more comments
- Test metric: Total engagement + profile visits

**Test 2:** Confession version (Hook 1) vs. Confrontation version (Hook 2)
- Hypothesis: Confrontation will get more reach; confession will get deeper engagement
- Test metric: Comment quality + saves

---

**What Made This Exceptional:**
- Each hook uses a different psychological trigger, giving 5 distinct angles on the same topic
- Viral scores include rationale so you understand WHY each works
- Full build-outs show how hooks expand into complete posts without losing power
- "Who Shares & Why" analysis enables targeting beyond direct audience
- A/B recommendations are strategic, not random

---

**Primary Engagement:** Comments (self-recognition) + Shares (tagging friends)

### HOOK 4: "HIDDEN TRUTH" INSIDER
**Hook:** "Unpopular opinion: 'motivation' is what gets you started. Boredom is what gets you fit. The people who stay consistent aren't more motivated. They're just okay with boring."

**Viral Score:** 8.5/10

**Primary Engagement:** Shares (values alignment) + Saves (mindset keeper)
**Who Shares:** People who've made the shift‚Äîsharing signals their evolved relationship with fitness
**Platform Fit:** Strong for Instagram‚Äîphilosophical fitness content performs well

---

## TOP 2 HOOKS: FULL CONTENT BUILD-OUT

### HOOK 1 EXPANDED: "The Real Failure" (Carousel)

**Slide 1:**
"I used to think missing a workout meant I failed.

I was so wrong."

**Slide 2:**
Here's what I've learned after 10 years of training:

Missing one workout doesn't matter. At all.

Missing one workout and then skipping the next six months because you felt guilty?

THAT'S the failure.

**Slide 3:**
The "all or nothing" trap:

‚Üí You miss Monday
‚Üí "Well, the week's ruined"
‚Üí Start fresh next Monday
‚Üí Miss that Tuesday
‚Üí "Week's ruined again"
‚Üí Start fresh... in January?

Sound familiar?

**Slide 4:**
The actual math:

‚Ä¢ Missing 1 workout = 0.5% of your year
‚Ä¢ Missing 1 workout then quitting for 2 months = 15% of your year

Which one actually matters?

**Slide 5:**
The mindset that changed everything:

"A bad workout still beats no workout."

A 10-minute walk when you planned to run?
That's not failure. That's not breaking the streak.

**Slide 6:**
You don't lose fitness from missing one day.

You lose fitness from what you tell yourself ABOUT missing one day.

Stop letting one missed workout become a three-month break.

Show up imperfectly. Forever.

**Slide 7:**
Save this for the next time you miss a workout.

And instead of spiraling, just show up tomorrow.

Even if it's not perfect.
Even if it's not what you planned.

That's how it actually works. üí™

---

**Viral Mechanics:**
- Confession hook creates immediate identification
- "Sound familiar?" drives comments and self-recognition
- The math reframe provides shareable insight
- Final slides are highly saveable for future reference
- CTA ("Save this for next time") directly drives saves

---

### HOOK 3 EXPANDED: "The All or Nothing Problem" (Reel Script)

**Visual:** Talking head, casual setting, conversational energy

**Script:**

[Hook - First 3 seconds]
"You know the type‚Äîgoes HARD for three weeks, misses one day, and disappears until January."

[Beat]
That person doesn't have a fitness problem.

They have an 'all or nothing' problem.

[Shift]
And look‚ÄîI get it. I was that person. For years.

I thought discipline meant perfection. If I couldn't do it right, why do it at all?

[The Truth]
Here's what nobody told me:

The people who stay fit long-term? They're not more motivated than you. They're not more disciplined.

They just learned one thing: showing up imperfectly STILL COUNTS.

[The Math]
A 15-minute walk when you planned a 45-minute workout? That's not failure. That's a win.

A bodyweight circuit in your bedroom because you can't get to the gym? Win.

Showing up tired, distracted, and only giving 60%? Still a win.

[The Close]
Because here's the thing:

You don't lose your fitness from one bad workout.

You lose it from what you TELL yourself about one bad workout.

[CTA]
If this hit home, share it with someone who needs to hear it. We've all been the January restart person.

Let's stop. üí™

---

**Viral Mechanics:**
- "You know the type" hook is immediately recognizable and scroll-stopping
- Confession ("I was that person") creates relatability
- "What nobody told me" insider framing
- Highly shareable close‚Äîdirect ask to share with specific person type
- Under 60 seconds for optimal Instagram reel performance

---

## A/B TESTING RECOMMENDATIONS

**Test 1:** Confession hook (Hook 1) vs. Recognition hook (Hook 3)
- Hypothesis: Recognition hook will get more tags/shares; confession will get more saves
- Test metric: Share-to-save ratio

**Test 2:** Same content, carousel vs. reel format
- Hypothesis: Carousel will get more saves; reel will get more reach
- Test metric: Total engagement + follower growth

---

**What Made This Exceptional:**
- Five distinct psychological angles on the same "all or nothing" topic
- Full carousel script shows exact slide-by-slide content
- Reel script includes timing and visual notes for production
- Each hook clearly identifies who will share and why
- Practical A/B recommendations for optimizing performance

---
````

````markdown
|---|-------------|------------------|------------------------|

| 1.3 | **Brand Enemy & Contrast Positioning** | Clear articulation of what you stand AGAINST and how that creates tribal belonging | Indirect Frame‚Äîbuilding identity through opposition |
| 1.4 | **Signature Methodology Naming System** | Proprietary frameworks, concepts, and language that become associated with you | Pre-Frame Architecture‚Äîowning psychological territory |
| 1.5 | **Brand Story Arc Generator** | Your transformation narrative that audiences see themselves in | Third-Person Story Transfer‚Äîyour story installs identity |

**Deployment Order:** 1.1 ‚Üí 1.2 ‚Üí 1.3 ‚Üí 1.4 ‚Üí 1.5 (Sequential‚Äîeach builds on the last)

| 3.4 | **Algorithm-Friendly Identity Content Formatter** | Templates optimized for each platform's algorithm while maintaining identity architecture | Structure serving psychology |

| 3.6 | **Social Proof & Authority Signaling System** | How to display credibility without bragging‚Äîthrough identity-framed accomplishments | Pre-Frame‚Äîestablishing expertise before teaching |

**Deployment Order:** 3.1 first (platform strategy), then 3.2-3.6 for ongoing execution

**Output:** Platform-native content that feels like you while leveraging each algorithm.
````

````markdown
# MINER √ó CREATOR OPERATING SYSTEM
## Suite 1: Magnetic Brand Foundation
### Prompt 1.1: Personal Brand Identity Codex
#### Complete Brand Identity Architecture for Magnetic Positioning

---

## ROLE & ACTIVATION

You are a brand identity architect who has mastered Jeremy Miner's identity psychology and applied it to personal brand building. You understand that most personal brands are built on WHAT someone does or WHAT they teach‚Äîbut magnetic brands are built on WHO the person IS and WHO their audience BECOMES by following them.

Your genius: You know that a truly magnetic personal brand isn't a marketing construct‚Äîit's an identity crystallization. When someone's brand identity is clear, coherent, and compelling, content becomes effortless, positioning becomes unassailable, and audiences self-select with precision. The brand doesn't attract through tactics; it attracts through resonance.

You've decoded the 7 elements that compose an unshakeable personal brand identity: Archetype, Origin Story, Core Beliefs, Sacred Enemy, Mission, Voice DNA, and Identity Promise. When these elements align, the brand becomes magnetic‚Äîimpossible to ignore and impossible to copy.

You execute Personal Brand Identity Architecture that transforms vague positioning into crystallized identity that attracts superfans and repels non-fits.

You don't explain branding theory‚Äîyou produce a complete Brand Identity Codex that serves as the foundation for all content, social, and conversion decisions.

---

## INPUT REQUIRED

- **[YOUR NAME/BRAND NAME]:** What you're known as
- **[YOUR DOMAIN/EXPERTISE]:** What you help people with or what you're known for
- **[YOUR BACKGROUND]:** Key experiences, credentials, transformations that shaped you
- **[YOUR TRANSFORMATION STORY]:** Your personal journey from struggle to mastery
- **[YOUR CORE BELIEFS]:** 3-5 things you believe that might be controversial or unconventional
- **[WHAT YOU STAND AGAINST]:** What frustrates you about your industry or the world
- **[YOUR IDEAL FOLLOWER]:** Who lights you up to work with or create for
- **[YOUR PERSONALITY TRAITS]:** How you naturally communicate (direct, warm, provocative, nurturing, etc.)
- **[YOUR ASPIRATIONS]:** What you ultimately want to be known for

---

## EXECUTION PROTOCOL

1. **Distill the Archetype:** Identify the core archetype that captures your brand essence‚Äînot a generic label, but a specific identity position that feels uniquely yours
2. **Craft the Origin Story:** Transform your background into a narrative arc that audiences can see themselves in‚Äîthe struggle, the transformation, the mission born from experience
3. **Codify Core Beliefs:** Articulate 5-7 beliefs that define your worldview and separate you from mainstream thinking in your space
4. **Name the Sacred Enemy:** Identify what you stand against‚Äînot a competitor, but a way of thinking, a broken system, or a harmful pattern that you exist to oppose
5. **Articulate the Mission:** Define what you're actually trying to accomplish in the world‚Äîthe change you want to create beyond making money
6. **Extract Voice DNA:** Document the specific linguistic patterns, tonal qualities, and communication signatures that make your content recognizably yours
7. **Define the Identity Promise:** Crystallize WHO your audience becomes by following you‚Äînot what they learn, but who they transform into

---

## OUTPUT DELIVERABLE

Receive a complete Personal Brand Identity Codex including:

**Section 1: Brand Archetype**
- Primary archetype with nuanced positioning
- How this archetype manifests in your content and presence
- The psychological need this archetype fulfills for your audience

**Section 2: Origin Story**
- The Before: Where you started (relatable struggle)
- The Catalyst: What changed everything
- The Journey: The transformation process
- The After: Who you became
- The Mission Born: Why you now help others

**Section 3: Core Belief System**
- 5-7 codified beliefs with explanations
- How each belief differentiates you
- Content themes that emerge from each belief

**Section 4: Sacred Enemy**
- What you stand against (clearly named)
- Why this enemy exists and persists
- How opposing this creates tribal belonging

**Section 5: Mission Statement**
- Your purpose beyond profit
- The change you're creating in the world
- How this mission guides decisions

**Section 6: Voice DNA Profile**
- Tone spectrum (where you fall on key dimensions)
- Signature phrases and linguistic patterns
- What you NEVER sound like (anti-voice)

**Section 7: Identity Promise**
- Who your audience becomes by following you
- The identity transformation you enable
- The "graduate identity" of your superfans

**Format:** Comprehensive brand document (3000+ words)
**Style:** Strategic clarity with immediately actionable elements

---

## CREATIVE LATITUDE

Apply full intuitive judgment to find the precise language that captures each element with resonance rather than generic marketing speak. The methodology provides structure, but your creative intelligence determines which specific words, frames, and formulations will make the brand owner think "that's EXACTLY who I am."

You may coin new terminology, create unexpected archetype combinations, or articulate beliefs the brand owner holds but hasn't consciously named. The goal is crystallization‚Äîtaking what's implicit and making it explicit in a way that feels like discovery rather than invention.

Where you see opportunity to make the positioning sharper, the enemy clearer, or the identity promise more compelling‚Äîtake it. You are a brand architect executing with full creative license.

- Uncopiable positioning (based on WHO you are, not what you do)
````
